CLASS LOADER ISOLATION:\\n- PluginClassLoader (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginClassLoader.java): Provides isolated class loading for individual plugins\\n- DelegatingClassLoader (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/DelegatingClassLoader.java): Manages multiple plugin class loaders and delegates class loading\\n- LoaderSwap (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/LoaderSwap.java): Handles context class loader swapping for plugin execution\\n- ClassLoaderFactory (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ClassLoaderFactory.java): Factory for creating delegating class loaders\\n- PluginClassLoaderFactory (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginClassLoaderFactory.java): Factory for creating plugin-specific class loaders\\n\\n2. PLUGIN SCANNING & DISCOVERY:\\n- PluginScanner (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginScanner.java): Abstract interface defining plugin discovery\\n- ReflectionScanner (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ReflectionScanner.java): Uses ClassGraph reflection to discover plugins in classpath\\n- ServiceLoaderScanner (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ServiceLoaderScanner.java): Uses Java ServiceLoader mechanism for plugin discovery\\n- PluginDiscoveryMode (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginDiscoveryMode.java): Configures which discovery strategies to use\\n- PluginScanResult (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginScanResult.java): Holds results of plugin scanning\\n- PluginSource (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginSource.java): Represents a source of plugins (JAR files in plugin paths)\\n\\n3. PLUGIN METADATA & UTILITIES:\\n- PluginDesc (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginDesc.java): Describes a discovered plugin (class name, version, type)\\n- PluginType (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginType.java): Enum of plugin types (CONNECTOR, CONVERTER, HEADER_CONVERTER, TRANSFORMATION, PREDICATE, etc.)\\n- PluginUtils (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginUtils.java): Utility methods for plugin path handling and location resolution\\n- PluginsRecommenders (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginsRecommenders.java): Provides recommendations for available plugins\\n- VersionedPluginLoadingException (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/VersionedPluginLoadingException.java): Exception for versioned plugin loading failures\\n\\n4. DEPENDENCY INJECTION & INSTANTIATION (Plugins.java):\\n- Plugins (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/Plugins.java): Central class implementing dependency injection for all plugin types. Key methods:\\n  - newConnector(String connectorClassOrAlias, VersionRange range): Creates connector instances\\n  - newConverter(AbstractConfig config, String classPropertyName): Creates converter instances\\n  - newHeaderConverter(AbstractConfig config, String classPropertyName): Creates header converter instances\\n  - newPlugin(String klassName, AbstractConfig config, Class<T> pluginKlass): Generic plugin instantiation\\n  - newTask(Class<? extends Task> taskClass): Creates task instances\\n  - newConfigProvider(): Creates config provider instances\\n  - Implements configuration injection via org.apache.kafka.common.Configurable.configure()\\n\\n5. PLUGIN INTERFACES (in connect/api):\\n- Connector (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/connector/Connector.java): Abstract base class for all connectors\\n- SinkConnector (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/sink/SinkConnector.java): Extends Connector for sink implementations\\n- SourceConnector (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/source/SourceConnector.java): Extends Connector for source implementations\\n- Converter (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/Converter.java): Interface for data converters\\n- HeaderConverter (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/HeaderConverter.java): Interface extending Configurable for header converters\\n- Transformation (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/transforms/Transformation.java): Interface for record transformations, extends Configurable\\n- Predicate (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/transforms/predicates/Predicate.java): Interface for transformation predicates\\n- ConnectRestExtension (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/rest/ConnectRestExtension.java): Interface for REST extension plugins\\n- ConnectorClientConfigOverridePolicy (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/connector/policy/ConnectorClientConfigOverridePolicy.java): Interface for config override policies\\n- Task (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/connector/Task.java): Base interface for tasks\\n- Versioned (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/components/Versioned.java): Interface for versioned components\\n\\n6. CONFIGURATION & VALIDATION:\\n- Configurable (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/Configurable.java): Core interface used for dependency injection - all plugin types implement this\\n- ConfigProvider (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/config/provider/ConfigProvider.java): Interface for external configuration providers\\n- ConverterConfig (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/ConverterConfig.java): Configuration for converters\\n- ConverterType (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/ConverterType.java): Enum for converter types (KEY, VALUE, HEADER)\\n- InstantiableClassValidator (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/util/InstantiableClassValidator.java): Validates classes have public no-arg constructors\\n- ConcreteSubClassValidator (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/util/ConcreteSubClassValidator.java): Validates classes are concrete subclasses\\n\\nARCHITECTURE FLOW:\\n1. Plugin Discovery: ReflectionScanner and ServiceLoaderScanner scan plugin paths and classpath\\n2. Plugin Metadata: Discovered plugins are stored as PluginDesc objects in PluginScanResult\\n3. Class Loading: DelegatingClassLoader installs discovered plugins and creates isolated PluginClassLoaders\\n4. Dependency Injection: Plugins class uses ClassLoader to instantiate plugin classes and calls Configurable.configure() with provided configuration\\n5. Isolation: LoaderSwap ensures plugin code executes with correct class loader context\\n\\nThe system supports multiple plugin types (Connectors, Converters, HeaderConverters, Transformations, Predicates, ConfigProviders, etc.) and enables version-specific plugin loading with fallback mechanisms.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":380,"cache_read_input_tokens":54502,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":380},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"78bbf92c-abea-40b4-b0e1-7f73ffedb5f6","uuid":"6e852ee1-0df0-45ba-a25a-e92425efef08"}

sophisticated class loader isolation and plugin discovery architecture. The core components are located in the org.apache.kafka.connect.runtime.isolation package.\\n\\nKey Components:\\n\\n1. CLASS LOADER ISOLATION:\\n- PluginClassLoader (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginClassLoader.java): Provides isolated class loading for individual plugins\\n- DelegatingClassLoader (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/DelegatingClassLoader.java): Manages multiple plugin class loaders and delegates class loading\\n- LoaderSwap (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/LoaderSwap.java): Handles context class loader swapping for plugin execution\\n- ClassLoaderFactory (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ClassLoaderFactory.java): Factory for creating delegating class loaders\\n- PluginClassLoaderFactory (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginClassLoaderFactory.java): Factory for creating plugin-specific class loaders\\n\\n2. PLUGIN SCANNING & DISCOVERY:\\n- PluginScanner (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginScanner.java): Abstract interface defining plugin discovery\\n- ReflectionScanner (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ReflectionScanner.java): Uses ClassGraph reflection to discover plugins in classpath\\n- ServiceLoaderScanner (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ServiceLoaderScanner.java): Uses Java ServiceLoader mechanism for plugin discovery\\n- PluginDiscoveryMode (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginDiscoveryMode.java): Configures which discovery strategies to use\\n- PluginScanResult (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginScanResult.java): Holds results of plugin scanning\\n- PluginSource (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginSource.java): Represents a source of plugins (JAR files in plugin paths)\\n\\n3. PLUGIN METADATA & UTILITIES:\\n- PluginDesc (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginDesc.java): Describes a discovered plugin (class name, version, type)\\n- PluginType (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginType.java): Enum of plugin types (CONNECTOR, CONVERTER, HEADER_CONVERTER, TRANSFORMATION, PREDICATE, etc.)\\n- PluginUtils (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginUtils.java): Utility methods for plugin path handling and location resolution\\n- PluginsRecommenders (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginsRecommenders.java): Provides recommendations for available plugins\\n- VersionedPluginLoadingException (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/VersionedPluginLoadingException.java): Exception for versioned plugin loading failures\\n\\n4. DEPENDENCY INJECTION & INSTANTIATION (Plugins.java):\\n- Plugins (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/Plugins.java): Central class implementing dependency injection for all plugin types. Key methods:\\n  - newConnector(String connectorClassOrAlias, VersionRange range): Creates connector instances\\n  - newConverter(AbstractConfig config, String classPropertyName): Creates converter instances\\n  - newHeaderConverter(AbstractConfig config, String classPropertyName): Creates header converter instances\\n  - newPlugin(String klassName, AbstractConfig config, Class<T> pluginKlass): Generic plugin instantiation\\n  - newTask(Class<? extends Task> taskClass): Creates task instances\\n  - newConfigProvider(): Creates config provider instances\\n  - Implements configuration injection via org.apache.kafka.common.Configurable.configure()\\n\\n5. PLUGIN INTERFACES (in connect/api):\\n- Connector (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/connector/Connector.java): Abstract base class for all connectors\\n- SinkConnector (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/sink/SinkConnector.java): Extends Connector for sink implementations\\n- SourceConnector (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/source/SourceConnector.java): Extends Connector for source implementations\\n- Converter (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/Converter.java): Interface for data converters\\n- HeaderConverter (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/HeaderConverter.java): Interface extending Configurable for header converters\\n- Transformation (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/transforms/Transformation.java): Interface for record transformations, extends Configurable\\n- Predicate (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/transforms/predicates/Predicate.java): Interface for transformation predicates\\n- ConnectRestExtension (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/rest/ConnectRestExtension.java): Interface for REST extension plugins\\n- ConnectorClientConfigOverridePolicy (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/connector/policy/ConnectorClientConfigOverridePolicy.java): Interface for config override policies\\n- Task (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/connector/Task.java): Base interface for tasks\\n- Versioned (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/components/Versioned.java): Interface for versioned components\\n\\n6. CONFIGURATION & VALIDATION:\\n- Configurable (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/Configurable.java): Core interface used for dependency injection - all plugin types implement this\\n- ConfigProvider (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/config/provider/ConfigProvider.java): Interface for external configuration providers\\n- ConverterConfig (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/ConverterConfig.java): Configuration for converters\\n- ConverterType (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/ConverterType.java): Enum for converter types (KEY, VALUE, HEADER)\\n- InstantiableClassValidator (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/util/InstantiableClassValidator.java): Validates classes have public no-arg constructors\\n- ConcreteSubClassValidator (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/util/ConcreteSubClassValidator.java): Validates classes are concrete subclasses\\n\\nARCHITECTURE FLOW:\\n1. Plugin Discovery: ReflectionScanner and ServiceLoaderScanner scan plugin paths and classpath\\n2. Plugin Metadata: Discovered plugins are stored as PluginDesc objects in PluginScanResult\\n3. Class Loading: DelegatingClassLoader installs discovered plugins and creates isolated PluginClassLoaders\\n4. Dependency Injection: Plugins class uses ClassLoader to instantiate plugin classes and calls Configurable.configure() with provided configuration\\n5. Isolation: LoaderSwap ensures plugin code executes with correct class loader context\\n\\nThe system supports multiple plugin types (Connectors, Converters, HeaderConverters, Transformations, Predicates, ConfigProviders, etc.) and enables version-specific plugin loading with fallback mechanisms.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

The core components are located in the org.apache.kafka.connect.runtime.isolation package.\\n\\nKey Components:\\n\\n1. CONFIGURATION & VALIDATION:\\n- Configurable (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/Configurable.java): Core interface used for dependency injection - all plugin types implement this\\n- ConfigProvider (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/config/provider/ConfigProvider.java): Interface for external configuration providers\\n- ConverterConfig (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/ConverterConfig.java): Configuration for converters\\n- ConverterType (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/ConverterType.java): Enum for converter types (KEY, VALUE, HEADER)\\n- InstantiableClassValidator (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/util/InstantiableClassValidator.java): Validates classes have public no-arg constructors\\n- ConcreteSubClassValidator (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/util/ConcreteSubClassValidator.java): Validates classes are concrete subclasses\\n\\nARCHITECTURE FLOW:\\n1. Plugin Discovery: ReflectionScanner and ServiceLoaderScanner scan plugin paths and classpath\\n2. Plugin Metadata: Discovered plugins are stored as PluginDesc objects in PluginScanResult\\n3. Class Loading: DelegatingClassLoader installs discovered plugins and creates isolated PluginClassLoaders\\n4. Dependency Injection: Plugins class uses ClassLoader to instantiate plugin classes and calls Configurable.configure() with provided configuration\\n5. Isolation: LoaderSwap ensures plugin code executes with correct class loader context\\n\\nThe system supports multiple plugin types (Connectors, Converters, HeaderConverters, Transformations, Predicates, ConfigProviders, etc.) and enables version-specific plugin loading with fallback mechanisms.\"\n}\n","numLines":75,"startLine":1,"totalLines":75}}}
